# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`

# Task: Implement PolicyQuotaController for Cilium

## Objective
Create a `PolicyQuotaController` in Cilium that enforces per-namespace limits on the
number of `CiliumNetworkPolicy` resources, preventing policy sprawl in multi-tenant clusters.

## Requirements

1. **Create `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`** with:
   - `PolicyQuotaController` struct that watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
   - `NewPolicyQuotaController(client, informer, maxPerNamespace int)` constructor
   - `Run(ctx context.Context)` method implementing the controller loop
   - Per-namespace counting using a thread-safe map
   - `CheckQuota(namespace string) error` method that returns error if quota exceeded

2. **Create CRD type** `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_policy_quota.go`:
   - `CiliumPolicyQuota` struct with `Spec.MaxPoliciesPerNamespace` field
   - Follow existing Cilium CRD patterns (DeepCopy, runtime.Object)

3. **Create `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go`** with tests

4. **Follow Cilium patterns**:
   - Use `hive` dependency injection framework
   - Use `resource.Resource[T]` for watching K8s resources
   - Use `logfields` for structured logging

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/policy/k8s/watcher.go` — CiliumNetworkPolicy watcher pattern
- `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_cnp.go` — CiliumNetworkPolicy CRD type
- `operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/` — controller using hive pattern
- `pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go` — resource watching framework

## Success Criteria
- PolicyQuotaController struct with Run method exists
- CheckQuota method performs namespace counting
- CiliumPolicyQuota CRD type exists
- Uses Cilium's hive/resource patterns
- Test file exists with test functions

    33→}

    38→	cnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],
    39→	policyQuotaResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumPolicyQuota],
    40→	maxPerNamespace int,

    44→		cnpResource:         cnpResource,
    45→		policyQuotaResource: policyQuotaResource,

    18→// per namespace.

93-usertool_resultRead
   100→		pc.incrementNamespaceCount(namespace)
   101→	case resource.Delete:
   102→		// Decrement policy count for namespace
   103→		pc.decrementNamespaceCount(namespace)
   104→	}
   105→}
   106→
   107→// handleQuotaEvent processes events for CiliumPolicyQuota resources.
   108→func (pc *PolicyQuotaController) handleQuotaEvent(event resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumPolicyQuota]) {
   109→	defer event.Done(nil)
   110→
   111→	if event.Kind == resource.Sync {
   112→		pc.log.Debug("PolicyQuota resources synced")
   113→		return
   114→	}
   115→
   116→	quota := event.Object
   117→	if quota == nil {
   118→		return
   119→	}
   120→
   121→	pc.mu.Lock()
   122→	if event.Kind == resource.Upsert {
   123→		// Update max policies per namespace if quota is updated
   124→		pc.maxPerNamespace = int(quota.Spec.MaxPoliciesPerNamespace)
   125→		pc.log.WithField("maxPerNamespace", pc.maxPerNamespace).
   126→			Debug("Updated maximum policies per namespace")
   127→	}
   128→	pc.mu.Unlock()
   129→}
   130→
   131→// CheckQuota checks if adding a new policy would exceed the quota for the given namespace.
   132→func (pc *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {
   133→	pc.mu.RLock()
   134→	defer pc.mu.RUnlock()
   135→
   136→	count, _ := pc.namespacePolicyCounts.LoadOrStore(namespace, 0)
   137→	currentCount := count.(int)
   138→
   139→	if currentCount >= pc.maxPerNamespace {
   140→		return fmt.Errorf("policy quota exceeded for namespace %s: current=%d, max=%d",
   141→			namespace, currentCount, pc.maxPerNamespace)
   142→	}
   143→	return nil
   144→}
   145→

   147→func (pc *PolicyQuotaController) incrementNamespaceCount(namespace string) {
   148→	val, _ := pc.namespac

// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package v2

import (
	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
)

// +genclient
// +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object
// +deepequal-gen:private-method=true
// +kubebuilder:resource:categories={cilium},singular="ciliumpolicyquota",path="ciliumpolicyquotas",scope="Namespaced",shortName={cpq}
// +kubebuilder:printcolumn:JSONPath=".metadata.creationTimestamp",name="Age",type=date
// +kubebuilder:storageversion

// CiliumPolicyQuota is a Kubernetes third-party resource for defining policy quotas
// per namespace.
type CiliumPolicyQuota struct {
	// +deepequal-gen=false
	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
	// +deepequal-gen=false
	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata"`

	// Spec is the desired policy quota specification.
	Spec CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
}

// +deepequal-gen=true

// CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec defines the policy quota specification.
type CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec struct {
	// MaxPoliciesPerNamespace is the maximum number of CiliumNetworkPolicy
	// resources allowed in a single namespace.
	//
	// +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=1
	// +kubebuilder:validation:Required
	MaxPoliciesPerNamespace int32 `json:"maxPoliciesPerNamespace"`
}

// +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object

// CiliumPolicyQuotaList is a list of CiliumPolicyQuota objects.
type CiliumPolicyQuotaList struct {
	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
	metav1.ListMeta `json:"metadata"`

	// Items is a list of CiliumPolicyQuota.
	Items []CiliumPolicyQuota `json:"items"`
}

// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0

package quota

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"sync"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	cilium_v2 "github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/resource"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
)

var (
	log = logrus.WithFields(logrus.Fields{
		logfields.LogSubsys: "policy-quota",
	})
)

// PolicyQuotaController manages per-namespace limits on the number of
// CiliumNetworkPolicy resources.
type PolicyQuotaController struct {
	log                  logrus.FieldLogger
	cnpResource          resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]
	policyQuotaResource  resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumPolicyQuota]
	maxPerNamespace      int
	namespacePolicyCounts sync.Map // map[string]int - namespace to policy count
	mu                   sync.RWMutex
}

// NewPolicyQuotaController creates a new PolicyQuotaController.
func NewPolicyQuotaController(
	logger logrus.FieldLogger,
	cnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],
	policyQuotaResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumPolicyQuota],
	maxPerNamespace int,
) *PolicyQuotaController {
	return &PolicyQuotaController{
		log:                 logger,
		cnpResource:         cnpResource,
		policyQuotaResource: policyQuotaResource,
		maxPerNamespace:     maxPerNamespace,
	}
}

// Run starts the controller loop that watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
// and tracks policy counts per namespace.
func (pc *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) {
	pc.log.Info("Starting PolicyQuotaController")

	// Watch both CNP and PolicyQuota resources
	cnpEvents := pc.cnpResource.Events(ctx)
	quotaEvents := pc.policyQuotaResource.Events(ctx)

	for {
		select {
		case <-ctx.Done():
			pc.log.Info("Stopping P

// MockResource implements a mock of resource.Resource[T] for testing
type MockResource[T any] struct {
	events chan resource.Event[T]
}

func NewMockResource[T any]() *MockResource[T] {
	return &MockResource[T]{
		events: make(chan resource.Event[T], 100),
	}
}

func (m *MockResource[T]) Events(ctx context.Context, opts ...resource.EventsOpt) <-chan resource.Event[T] {
	return m.events
}

func (m *MockResource[T]) Observe(ctx context.Context, next func(resource.Event[T]) error, complete func(error)) error {
	return nil
}

func (m *MockResource[T]) Store(ctx context.Context) (resource.Store[T], error) {
	return nil, nil
}

func (m *MockResource[T]) SendEvent(event resource.Event[T]) {
	select {
	case m.events <- event:
	default:
		// Channel full, discard
	}
}

// MockEvent implements resource.Event[T]
type MockEvent[T any] struct {
	kind   resource.EventKind
	object T
}

func (e *MockEvent[T]) Kind() resource.EventKind {
	return e.kind
}

func (e *MockEvent[T]) Object() T {
	return e.object
}

func (e *MockEvent[T]) Done(err error) {
	// No-op for mock
}

# PolicyQuotaController Implementation Summary

## Overview
Successfully implemented a `PolicyQuotaController` for Cilium that enforces per-namespace limits on the number of `CiliumNetworkPolicy` resources, preventing policy sprawl in multi-tenant clusters.

## Files Created

### 1. CRD Type Definition
**File**: `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_policy_quota.go`

Defines the `CiliumPolicyQuota` Kubernetes CRD with:
- `CiliumPolicyQuota` struct with:
  - `TypeMeta` for Kubernetes object metadata
  - `ObjectMeta` for name, namespace, labels, etc.
  - `Spec` containing `MaxPoliciesPerNamespace`
- `CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec` with `MaxPoliciesPerNamespace: int32` field
- `CiliumPolicyQuotaList` for list operations
- Proper kubebuilder annotations for CRD generation
- DeepCopy support through annotations

**Key Features**:
- Scoped to Namespaced resources
- Path: `ciliumpolicyquotas`
- Short name: `cpq`
- Validation: MaxPoliciesPerNamespace must be >= 1

### 2. PolicyQuotaController
**File**: `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`

Core controller implementation:

```go
type PolicyQuotaController struct {
    log                   logrus.FieldLogger
    cnpResource           resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]
    policyQuotaResource   resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumPolicyQuota]
    maxPerNamespace       int
    namespacePolicyCounts sync.Map // thread-safe namespace->count mapping
    mu                    sync.RWMutex
}
```

**Key Methods**:
- `NewPolicyQuotaController()` - Constructor
- `Run(ctx context.Context)` - Main controller loop
  - Watches both CNP and PolicyQuota resources
  - Handles Upsert/Delete/Sync events
  - Thread-safe event handling
- `CheckQuota(namespace string) error` - Checks if quota exceeded
  - Returns error if current count >= maxPerNamespac
... (truncated)
